create or replace PROCEDURE         "BRF2_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" ( REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 

  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 


BEGIN 



--14-GORVERMENT SECTOR-DEMAND (14.1)



UPDATE  BRF2_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF2', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW102' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='GS-Demand'
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE  IN  ('SGOVT')AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13101','13201', '13206', '13215', '13216', '13217', '13220','13241', '24301', '24311','24312', '24313', 
'24319', '24503', '24337')and  sol_id in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

--GORVERMENT SECTOR-SAVINGS (14.2)

UPDATE  BRF2_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF2', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW103' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='GS-Savings'
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE  IN  ('SGOVT')AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13217', '13220', '13421') and  sol_id in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

--GORVERMENT SECTOR-Time including CDs/ structured products (14.3)

UPDATE  BRF2_MAPPING_TABLE SET  REPORT_NAME_1 ='BRF2', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW104' , report_addl_criteria_1 ='GS-Time'
WHERE CONSTITUTION_CODE  IN  ('SGOVT')AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13241', '13601', '13611', '13631', '13641') and  sol_id in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008') AND report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

and GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE in ('13217', '13220', '13421') and  sol_id in ('9001','9002','9003','9004','9005','9008')
and report_date=V_REPORT_DATE;

---DETAIL PROCEDURE
create or replace PROCEDURE         "BRF2_DETAIL_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   v_report_date   date := to_date (report_date, 'DD-MON-YYYY');
BEGIN


delete from BRF2_DETAILTABLE where report_date = '30-jun-2023';
Commit;


insert into brf2_detailtable
(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,FORACID,NRE_FLG,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID)
select ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,ACCT_NAME,ACID,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,CUST_ID,FORACID,NRE_STATUS,REMARKS,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,SOL_ID from brf2_mapping_table 
where report_date='30-jun-2023' AND report_label_1 is not  null;



COMMIT;


END;
